---
title: "随机地下城"
source_collection: "DND五版不全书v2026.02.12"
book: "城主指南"

category: "legacy-core"

<div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>本附录可以帮你快速生成地下城。下列诸表格会频繁用到。首先，掷骰决定一个起始区域，再掷骰来确定在该地区发现的通道和门。有了初始的通道和门后，再确定之后的通道、门、房间、楼梯等等，而其中每项都由不同的表格掷骰得来。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>按照这里所述的方法可以制作出极其庞大的地下城，其设计可能填涂超过一张方格纸。而如果你想限制地城的大小<span lang="EN-US">,</span>就要提前设定它的扩张极限。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>对地下城大小最见效的限制就是确定其绘制所需的方格纸。地城的特征物一旦超过纸张边界就将其剔除。走廊可能会在地图边缘拐弯或出现死胡同，或者你也可以在剩余的空间里设定一个小房间以作填充。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>此外，你还可以将地图边缘的通道设定为另一个地下城的入口。楼梯、竖井和其他一些通往另一层域的特征物，在你不想再继续绘制本地图时也可以实现类似的作用。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">起始区域</span><span lang="EN-US">Starting Area</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>表格“起始区域”可以为你提供一个房间或一条设定好的通道作为通往地下城的入口。掷骰决定随机起始区域时，还要选定其中一扇门或通道作为起始区域通向地下城主体的入口。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>选定入口后，再按照对应的表格掷骰决定各通道和门口会将人从起始区域带往何处。每个通道将延伸至起始区域<span lang="EN-US">10</span>尺以外。到达该距离后，对照表格“通道”来确定每条通道后续部分的具体内容。使用表格“门后”来确定每扇门或密门后方的具体内容。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-family:黑体;color:black">起始区域</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">Starting Area</span>

|                                                 |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|-------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d10</span>**               | **<span style="font-family:黑体">配置</span>**                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

| <span lang="EN-US">4</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">长方形，</span><span lang="EN-US">80 x 20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺；中间有一排支柱；长边每面墙上各有一条通道，短边每面墙上各有一扇门</span>                       |

| <span lang="EN-US">6</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">圆形，直径</span><span lang="EN-US">40</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺；每个主要方向有一条通道</span>                                                                    |

| <span lang="EN-US">8</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">正方形，</span><span lang="EN-US">20 x 20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺；两面墙上有门，第三面墙上有通道，第四面墙上有密门</span>                                       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">9</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                       
                                                     color:black">通道，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">T</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;  
                                                     color:black">型路口</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span lang="EN-US">10</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">通道，</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺；十字路口</span>                                                                                      |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">通道</span><span lang="EN-US">Passages</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>生成通道和走廊时，对照表格“通道”进行多次掷骰，你可以在地图上任意延伸通道的长度或设置分支，直至其抵达一扇门或一个房间。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>每当生成新通道时，你都可以掷骰来决定它的宽度。如果该通道自另一通道分支处延伸而来，则根据表格“通道宽度”骰<span lang="EN-US">d12</span>来确定其宽度。如果通道是从房间延伸而来，按表格骰<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>来确定其宽度，但是该通道的宽度必须比该房间所在墙面的最长尺寸至少小<span lang="EN-US">5</span>尺。

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">通道</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Passage</span>

|                                                     |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
|-----------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                   | **<span style="font-family:黑体">细节</span>**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~2</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                         color:black">继续笔直延伸</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">30</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺，没有门或侧通道。</span>                                                                                                         |
| <span lang="EN-US">3</span>                         | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">继续笔直延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺，右侧有一扇门，再延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺</span>      |

                                                         color:black">尺</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| <span lang="EN-US">8~9</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">继续笔直延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺，左侧一条分道，再延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺</span>      |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">10</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                         color:black">继续笔直延伸</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺，进入死胡同，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">10%</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;         
                                                         color:black">几率有一扇密门</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US">11~12</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">继续笔直延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺，左拐，再延伸</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺</span>              |

                                                         color:black">楼梯</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">\*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">（按表格“楼梯”掷骰）</span>                                                                                                                 |

<span lang="EN-US">\*</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">楼梯的存在意味着地下城不止一层。如果你不想要一个多层的地下城，可以选择重骰，把楼梯作为其他地点的入口，或者直接用你选择的特征物进行替换。</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">门</span><span lang="EN-US">doors</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>每当掷骰结果生成门时，对照表格“门类型”来确定其样式，再对照表格“门后”掷骰确定门的后方有什么。如果一扇门被栓死，则由你决定栓在门的哪边。你也可以将未上锁的们设定为卡死。详见第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>章“冒险环境”里门与闸门相关内容。

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">门类型</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Door Type</span>

|                                                    |                                                                               |
|----------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                  | **<span style="font-family:黑体">门类型</span>**                              |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~10</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                        color:black">木质</span>                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">11~12</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">木质，栓住或上锁</span>   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">13</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                        color:black">石质</span>                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">14</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">石质，栓住或上锁</span>   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">15</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

| <span lang="EN-US">16</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">铁质，栓住或上锁</span>   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">17</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

| <span lang="EN-US">18</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">铁闸门，某处被锁死</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">19</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                        color:black">密门</span>                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">密门，栓住或上锁</span>   |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">房间</span><span lang="EN-US">Chambers</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>每当掷骰结果生成一个房间时，对照表格“房间”来确定其尺寸。再对照表格“房间出口”来确定出口的数量。然后对照表格“出口位置”和“出口类型”来确定出口的样式和位置。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>使用“填充地下城”一节中的表格来设定房间内部。

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">房间</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Chamber</span>

| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">5~6</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

| <span lang="EN-US">13~14</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">长方形，</span><span lang="EN-US">40 x 50</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺²</span>         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">15</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                        
                                                         color:black">长方形，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">50 x 80</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺²</span>               |
| <span lang="EN-US">16</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">圆形，直径</span><span lang="EN-US">30</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺¹</span>            |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">17</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                        
                                                         color:black">圆形，直径</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">50</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺²</span>                  |
| <span lang="EN-US">18</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">八边形，</span><span lang="EN-US">40 x 40</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺²</span>         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">19</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                        
                                                         color:black">八边形，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">60 x 60</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺²</span>               |
| <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">不规则四边形，约</span><span lang="EN-US">40 x 60</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺²</span> |

<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black;mso-color-alt:
windowtext">¹</span> <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">使用表格“房间出口”的普通房间栏</span><span lang="EN-US">  
</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">²</span> <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">使用表格“房间出口”的大型房间栏</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

| <span lang="EN-US">11~20</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">走廊，</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺长</span> |

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">楼梯</span><span lang="EN-US">Stairs</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>楼梯包括任何可以上楼或下楼的特征物，包括斜坡<span lang="EN-US">ramps</span>、烟囱<span lang="EN-US">chimneys</span>、开放的竖井<span lang="EN-US">shafts</span>、升降梯<span lang="EN-US">elevator</span>和爬梯<span lang="EN-US">ladders</span>。如果你的地下城不止一层，你可以在各层之间放置一定数量的楼梯。大多数地下城的楼梯可以定为<span lang="EN-US">30</span>尺距离。

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">楼梯</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Stairs</span>

|                                                   |                                                                                                                                                                                |
|---------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                 | **<span style="font-family:                                                                                                                                                    
                                                       黑体">楼梯</span>**                                                                                                                                                           |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~4</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">下降一层至一个房间</span>                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">5~8</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">下降一层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺通道</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">9</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">下降两层至一个房间</span>                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">10</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">下降两层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺通道</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">11</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">下降三层至一个房间</span>                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">12</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">下降三层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺通道</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">13</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">上升一层至一个房间</span>                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">14</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">上升一层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺通道</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">15</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">上升至一条死胡同</span>                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US">16</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">下降至一条死胡同</span>                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">17</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">从烟囱上升一层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺通道</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US">18</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">从烟囱上升两层至一条长</span><span lang="EN-US">20</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺通道</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">19</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                            
                                                       color:black">竖井（有或无升降梯）下降一层至一个房间</span>                                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">竖井（有或无升降梯）下降一层至一个房间，同时可上升一层至一个房间</span>                                                    |

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">连接区域</span><span lang="EN-US">Connecting Areas</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>你的地图完成后，可以再考虑在彼此相邻的房间和通道间添加门口，或是让其维持不相连的状态。这些门路可以创造更多穿越地下城的路径并扩展玩家们的选择。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>如果你的地下城包括不止一层的结构，则必须确保各层之间有连接的楼梯、陷坑和其他垂直的通道。如果你使用方格纸，则可以在当前地图上再该一页纸，标记好楼梯和其他连接两个层面特征物的位置，然后再开始绘制新层域的地图。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

## <span style="font-family:黑体">填充地下城</span><span lang="EN-US">Stocking a dungeon</span>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>制作自己的地下城地图只是这份乐趣的一半。完成规划图后，你就可以设定各地下城通道和房间里能发现什么挑战和奖励。任何合理的大型空间应充斥着有趣的景象、音响、物件以及生物。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>你不需要将地城中的每个细节都绘制出来。你可以制作一份怪物清单和一份宝藏清单，再用一份清单明每个地下城区域特有的一两个要素。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">房间用途</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Chamber Purpose</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>房间本身的用途可以帮助确定其内部家具和其他内容。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>为你的地城地图上每个房间分配用途，或使用下列表格来激发构思。每种类型的地城在第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>章节“冒险环境”的“地下城用途”中都有描述，同时它们也分别有自己的表格用以依据地下城用途来设置房间。例如，设计一座陵墓时可以使用表格“地下城：陵墓”来辅助设定房间用途。这些描述地下城详情的表格后面还有一张“通用地下城房间”表。该表可以用在你设计的地下城跟各标准类型不符，或是想混入一些其他东西的时候。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>让整个地城都依靠随机掷骰决定内容时，可能会出现一些不协调感。一个小房间可能最终被确定为一座神庙，而隔壁的巨大房间则仅仅被用作储藏室。虽然尝试为这种奇怪的配置安排合理解释也许会非常有趣，但是你最好还是对其作一些适当更改。你可以预留一些比较关键的房间，随后再专门为其作内容设定。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">地下城：死亡困境</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black"> Dungeon: Death Trap</span>

|                                                     |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|-----------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                   | **<span style="font-family:                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                
                                                         黑体">用途</span>**                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1</span>     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

                                                         color:black">，供观众使用</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US">2~8</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">警卫室</span><span lang="EN-US">guardroom</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">，被加固用以抵挡入侵者</span>                                                                                                                      |

                                                         color:black">的概率会被锁在里面）</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US">12~14</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">房间</span><span lang="EN-US">room</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">，内有一个谜题，必须将其解决才能绕过某个陷阱或怪物</span>                                                                                                 |

| <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">观察室</span><span lang="EN-US">observation room</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">，让警卫或观众得以观察地下城中各生物的移动状况</span>                                                                                       |

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<td width="13%" data-valign="top" style="width: 13.86%; background: #D9D9D9; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt; height: 1.0pt"><p><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span></p></td>
<td width="34%" data-valign="top" style="width: 34.0%; background: #D9D9D9; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt; height: 1.0pt"><p><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">room</span></p></td>

<td width="33%" data-valign="top" style="width: 33.32%; background: #D9D9D9; padding: 0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt; height: 1.0pt"><p><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;
  color:black">走廊</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">hallway</span></p></td>

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">房间现状</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Current Chamber State</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>如果一个地下城曾经历一段动荡的历史，那么你可以掷骰确定某个特定区域的现状。不过，如果该房间仍然用于实现其预定的用途，则表示其完好无损。

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">房间现状</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Current Chamber State</span>

|                                                     |                                                                               |
|-----------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                   | **<span style="font-family:黑体">特征物</span>**                              |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~3</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                         color:black">瓦砾，天花板部分倒塌</span>                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">4~5</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">坑洞，地面部分倒塌</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">6~7</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                         color:black">灰烬，主要是燃烧所致</span>                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">8~9</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">用作一个营地</span>       |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">10~11</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                         color:black">一池水；房间原本的内容物被水毁坏</span>                         |
| <span lang="EN-US">12~16</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">家具受损但仍然存在</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">17~18</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                         color:black">转为作其他用途（骰表格“通用地下城房间”）</span>                 |
| <span lang="EN-US">19</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">空无一物</span>           |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">20</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                           
                                                         color:black">维持原状且光洁如新</span>                                       |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">房间内容</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Chamber Contents</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>你对各地下城内各房间的用途有一个整体印象后，就可以考虑为这些区域填充具体的内容。表格“地下城房间内容”可以用来随机掷骰决定房间里的内容，或者你也可以自选特定区域的内容。如果你决定自行选择内容，则务必让其包含丰富多彩的各种有趣东西。除该表所示内容外，本附录提及的“地下城装饰”也提供了其他的物品和要素来填充房间。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>表格“地下城房间内容”中，“主要生物”表示一个控制该区域的生物。宠物与结盟生物屈从于主要生物。“随机生物”则是食腐动物或一些生物公害，它们通常都是经过该区域的单个怪物或小团体。这类生物包括食腐虫<span lang="EN-US">carrion crawlers</span>、恐鼠<span lang="EN-US">dire rats</span>、凝胶方块<span lang="EN-US">gelatimous cubes</span>和锈蚀怪<span lang="EN-US">rust monsters</span>等等。详见第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>章“创造冒险”来获取更多关于随机遭遇的信息。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">地下城房间内容</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Dungeon Chamber Contents</span>

|                                                     |                                                                                           |
|-----------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d100</span>**                  | **<span style="font-family:黑体">内容</span>**                                            |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">01~08</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">怪物（主要生物）</span>                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">09~15</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">怪物（主要生物）与宝藏</span>         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">16~27</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">怪物（宠物或结盟生物）</span>                                               |
| <span lang="EN-US">28~33</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">怪物（宠物或结盟生物）守护宝藏</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">34~42</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">怪物（随机生物）</span>                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">43~50</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">怪物（随机生物）与宝藏</span>         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">51~58</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">地下城危害物（见“随机地下城危害物”）附带次要宝藏</span>                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">59~63</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">障碍（见“随机障碍”）</span>           |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">64~73</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">陷阱（见“随机陷阱”）</span>                                                 |
| <span lang="EN-US">74~76</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">陷阱（见“随机陷阱”）保护宝藏</span>   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">77~80</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">唬人把戏（见“随机唬人把戏”）</span>                                         |
| <span lang="EN-US">81~88</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">空房间</span>                         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">89~94</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                       
                                                         color:black">空房间与地下城危害物（见“随机地下城危害物”）</span>                         |
| <span lang="EN-US">95~00</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">空房间附带宝藏</span>                 |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:black;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">怪物和动机</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Monster and Motivations</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>见第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>章“创建冒险”中关于创建与怪物相关遭遇的指引。为了促进多样化和悬念，请确保有出现不同难度的遭遇。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>进入地下城初期就遭遇一个强大的生物，可以促进兴奋感并迫使冒险者们开动脑筋。例如，一只远古红龙沉睡在地下城第一层，浓烟和他沉重的呼吸声充斥着其巢穴附近的房间。精明的角色将尽最大努力来避开龙，队伍里的大胆窃贼甚至还会顺带从那财宝堆中偷走一些钱币。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>并不是所有怪物都直接与玩家敌对。你的地下城中安排怪物时，可以思考一下它们与附近生物的关系，以及它们对冒险者的态度。角色们可以提供食物来安抚饥饿的野兽，而更聪明的生物则有更复杂的动机。表格“怪物动机”可以帮你赋予怪物一个目标来定义它在地下城中的存在。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>在复数的房间中都有遭遇的一大群怪物，其动机可能适用整个种族，其子群的目标还可能会存在某些冲突。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">怪物动机</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Monster Motivation</span>

|                                                   |                                                                       |                                 |                                                     |                                                                         |
|---------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                 | **<span style="font-family:黑体">目标</span>**                        | **<span lang="EN-US"> </span>** | **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                   | **<span style="font-family:黑体">目标</span>**                          |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~2</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                   
                                                       color:black">寻找一个避难所</span>                                   | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">12~13</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                       color:black">躲避敌人</span>                                           |
| <span lang="EN-US">3~5</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">征服地下城</span> | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US">14~15</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">从战斗中恢复</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">6~8</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                   
                                                       color:black">地下城中找一个物品</span>                               | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">16~17</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                       color:black">躲避危险</span>                                           |
| <span lang="EN-US">9~11</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">杀死对手</span>   | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US">18~20</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">寻求财富</span>     |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">随机地下城危害物</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Random Dungeon Hazards</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>怪物们会清除或避开危害物，因而栖息地区域很少出现这类东西。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>尖叫菌<span lang="EN-US">shriekers</span>和紫腐菌<span lang="EN-US">violet fungi</span>在*《怪物图鉴》*中有描述。表中其他危害物则在第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>章“冒险环境”中有描述。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">地下城危害物</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Dungeon Hazards</span>

|                                                    |                                                                                                        |                                 |                                                     |                                                                                                          |
|----------------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                  | **<span style="font-family:黑体">危害物</span>**                                                       | **<span lang="EN-US"> </span>** | **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                   | **<span style="font-family:黑体">危害物</span>**                                                         |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1~3</span>  | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                    
                                                        color:black">棕霉菌</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">brown mold</span>                    | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">11~15</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         color:black">蜘蛛网</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">spiderwebs</span>                      |
| <span lang="EN-US">4~8</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">绿软泥</span><span lang="EN-US">green slime</span> | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US">16~17</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">紫腐菌</span><span lang="EN-US">violet fungus</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">9~10</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                    
                                                        color:black">尖叫菌</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">shrieker</span>                      | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">18~20</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         color:black">黄霉菌</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">yellow mold</span>                     |

<span lang="EN-US" style="color:white;mso-color-alt:windowtext"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">随机障碍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Random Obstacles</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>障碍对穿越地下城的进程造成限制。某些情况下，冒险者们认为的障碍在地下城居民看来只是一条普通的通道。例如，一个半淹的房间对很多角色来说是一个障碍，但是对天生水下呼吸生物来说则是更轻松的地方。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>障碍可以影响不止复数的房间。一条裂谷可能横穿几条通道和几个房间，或者其裂缝沿着石艺加工的痕迹延伸到更广阔的周边地区。某区域的魔法祭坛升起猛烈的风流，并可能因此搅动空气而使四周百里之外区域的危险性降低。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">障碍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Obstacles</span>

|                                                    |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|----------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d20</span>**                  | **<span style="font-family:黑体">障碍</span>**                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1</span>    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                        color:black">防生物灵光覆盖一片半径</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1d10 x 10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺的区域；灵光内的活体生物不能回复生命值</span>                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US">2</span>                        | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">冲击的风会使移动速度减半，同时使远程攻击检定具有劣势</span>                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">3</span>    | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
                                                        color:black">剑刃护壁</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">blade barrier</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;color:black">堵住通道</span>                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US">4~8</span>                      | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">坍塌</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">9~12</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                        color:black">深沟，宽</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1d4 x 10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">尺，深</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">2d6 x 10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;  
                                                        color:black">尺，可能会连接到地下城的其他层域</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| <span lang="EN-US">13~14</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">淹没深度达</span><span lang="EN-US">2d10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">尺的区域；出现在向上倾斜的通道、上升的楼层或上升的楼梯等地，其附近必须有水</span>                                   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">15</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                        color:black">熔岩流经该地区（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">50%</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">几率有一座跨越熔岩的石桥）</span>                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US">16</span>                       | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">疯长的蘑菇挡住前路，必须将其砍伐才能通过（</span><span lang="EN-US">25%</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">几率有一片霉菌或真菌类危害物隐藏其中）</span>                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">17</span>   | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                        
                                                        color:black">有毒气体（暴露在其中的生物每分钟受</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1d6</span><span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;color:black">的毒素损伤）</span>                                                                                |
| <span lang="EN-US">18</span>                       | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">反转重力</span><span lang="EN-US">Reverse gravity</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">的效应使生物坠向天板</span>                                                                             |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">19</span>   | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                       
                                                        color:black">火墙术</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">wall of fire</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;color:black">堵住通道</span>                                                                                                     |
| <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                       | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">力场墙</span><span lang="EN-US">wall of force</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">堵住通道</span>                                                                                             |

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">随机陷阱</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Random Traps</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>如果你需要随手的陷阱或要在地下城中放置随机陷阱，可以使用第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>章“冒险环境”中提到的陷阱范例或下列表格。如果你选择使用表格，那么先使用表格“陷阱效应”和“陷阱触发”来设定陷阱的类型，再使用表格“陷阱危害度”来决定它的致命程度。关于陷阱危害度的更多信息，详见第<span lang="EN-US">5</span>章。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">陷阱触发</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Trap Trigger</span>

| <span lang="EN-US">2</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">走过（门道，过道）</span>   |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">3</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">随机唬人把戏</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Random Tricks</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>相比陷阱，唬人把戏并不致命而又离奇古怪。它们有些是地下城创造者遗留下的影响，有些则可能是弥漫地下城中奇特魔法能量的体现。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>下列表格可以帮你随机生成一些唬人把戏。先掷骰决定一个设置把戏的物件，再掷骰确定把戏的性质。一些唬人把戏是无法驱散的永久效应，另一些则是临时存在，或是可以被*解除魔法<span lang="EN-US">dispel magic</span>*抵消。具体状况随你设定。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">唬人物件</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Trick Objects</span>

| <span lang="EN-US">8</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">玻璃塑像</span>         | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US">18</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">护甲套装</span> |

| <span lang="EN-US">10</span>                    | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">油画</span>             | <span lang="EN-US"> </span>     | <span lang="EN-US">20</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">假人</span>     |

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">唬人把戏</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Tricks</span>

|                                                     |                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
|-----------------------------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| **<span lang="EN-US">d100</span>**                  | **<span style="font-family:黑体">唬人效应</span>**                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">01~03</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">使第一触碰物件的人衰老</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| <span lang="EN-US">04~06</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">使被触碰物件活化，或活化它附近的其他物件</span>                                                                                                                                                                              |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">07~10</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;

| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">14~16</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">触碰时改变角色的阵营、个性、体型、外貌或性别</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span lang="EN-US">17~19</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">将一种物质转变为另一种物质，比如黄金变成铅或金属变成易碎的水晶</span>                                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">20~22</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">生成一个力场</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span lang="EN-US">23~26</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">产生一个幻象</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">27~29</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">在一段时间里压制魔法物品</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US">30~32</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">变巨或缩小各角色</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">33~35</span> | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
                                                         color:black">魔嘴术</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">magic mouth</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;color:black">说出一个谜语</span>                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">36~38</span>                     | *<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">困惑术</span><span lang="EN-US">confusion</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">（指定</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">尺内的所有生物）</span> |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">39~41</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">指出方向（真或假）</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US">42~44</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">实现一个愿望</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">45~47</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">飞起来，以避免被触碰</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">48~50</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">对角色施展</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">指使术</span><span lang="EN-US">geas</span>*                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">51~53</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">加强，减弱，消除，或逆转重力</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span lang="EN-US">54~56</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">促进贪婪之心</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">57~59</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">收容一个被禁锢的生物</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US">60~62</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">锁定或解锁出口</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">63~65</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">提供一场可选的游戏，以此承诺一项奖励或一条有价值的情报</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| <span lang="EN-US">66~68</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">帮助或伤害特定类型的生物</span>                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">69~71</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                             
                                                         color:black">对角色们施展</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                            
                                                         color:black">变形术</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">polymorph</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;color:black">（持续</span><span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">1</span><span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;;             
                                                         color:black">小时）</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| <span lang="EN-US">72~75</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">出现一条谜题或谜语</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">76~78</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">阻止移动</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US">79~81</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">放出钱币，假钱币，宝石，假宝石，一件魔法物品，或地图</span>                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">82~84</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">放出，召唤，或变成一个怪物</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US">85~87</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;Heiti SC Light&quot;">对角色们施展</span>*<span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">暗示术</span><span lang="EN-US">suggestion</span>*                                                                                                  |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">88~90</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">触碰时会大声的哭喊</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| <span lang="EN-US">91~93</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">说话（正常讲演，废话，诗歌和童谣，唱歌，施法，或尖叫）</span>                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span lang="EN-US" style="color:black">94~97</span> | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;;                                                                                                                                                                                                                              
                                                         color:black">将角色们传送至另一个地方</span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span lang="EN-US">98~00</span>                     | <span style="font-family:&quot;STHeiti light&quot;">交换两名角色或多名角色的意识</span>                                                                                                                                                                                          |

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">随机宝藏</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Random Treasures</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>使用第<span lang="EN-US">7</span>章“宝藏”中的表格和指引，来设定地下城中各个区域的宝藏。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">空房间</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Empty Rooms</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>角色们需要一个安全地点进行短休时，一个空房间的出现俨然天赐之物。角色们也可以躲藏其内进行长休。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>这样的房间有时并不像看上去一样空荡。如果人物仔细搜寻房间，你可以给他们奖励一个密室，其中包含一个本先前居民的日记，一幅指向另一地下城的地图，或是其他的发现。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid #B79C61 1.0pt;padding:0cm 0cm 1.0pt 0cm">

**<span style="font-family:黑体;color:maroon">地下城装饰</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;color:maroon">Dungeon Dressing</span>**

</div>

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>本节的诸表格提供了可放置在地下城中的杂项物品和特征点。地下城装饰可以帮助营造地下城的氛围，提供一些关于它的创造者和历史的线索，为设置唬人把戏和陷阱提供基础，或以此鼓励玩家进行探索。<span lang="EN-US">  
</span>生成随机地下城装饰时，可以分别用下列的每个表格作一次掷骰：“声响”“空气”和“气味”。而本节的其他表格则可以随意进行多次掷骰，或直接从中选择合适的家具作摆设。

<span lang="EN-US"> </span>

#### <span style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:黑体;color:black">空气</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size:9.5pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif;color:black">Air</span>

                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              color:black">纯净且有清风吹过</span>                                       |
